策略指南：
- 战斗中，当敌人预告高伤害时优先格挡
- 构建牌组联动 —— 不要加入与你流派不搭的牌
- 高效管理能量 —— 优先打高价值牌
- 休息点：血量高于60%时优先升级而非休息
- 血量允许时优先打精英获取更好奖励
- 有机会时移除弱牌（打击）

- 药水留给硬仗（精英、Boss）—— 不要浪费在简单战斗上

Vicious only triggers once per turn though, which isn't that impactful. Molten Fist is the stronger pick—it's efficient damage output, self-exhausts to keep the deck lean, and synergizes nicely with Bash's vulnerable application.

Updated after: Run 1 (Ironclad, Ascension 0, Defeated by Waterfall Giant Boss at Floor 17)

== BOSS KNOWLEDGE ==
WATERFALL_GIANT:
- 250 HP, gains SteamEruptionPower (increases each turn, was 36 by end)
- CRITICAL: Has a SECOND PHASE after being "killed" — transforms to 999999999 HP and attacks for full SteamEruption damage
- You MUST have enough block to survive the steam eruption hit (36+ damage)
- Strategy: Need massive block preparation before killing. Don't rush the kill.
- Consider: Save block potions, build enough defense to tank the eruption turn
- Prioritize having 40+ HP when entering this fight
- The boss heals and buffs on some turns — use those to set up

== CARD COMBOS (PROVEN EFFECTIVE) ==
- Rupture + Bloodletting: Each Bloodletting triggers +1 strength from Rupture. Core engine.
- Bloodletting + Whirlwind: Extra energy = extra Whirlwind hits. Amazing burst.
- 2x Bloodletting + Whirlwind: 7 energy Whirlwind = 35+ base damage AoE
- Battle Trance + attack-heavy hand: 0-cost draw 3 maximizes energy efficiency
- Headbutt + key card retrieval: Search for Whirlwind/Bloodletting as needed
- Bash + Molten Fist: 2 vuln → doubled to 4 vuln, massive damage window
- Juggling + 3 attacks/turn: Free card copy, best with high-value attacks

== CARD EVALUATIONS ==
TOP TIER: Whirlwind, Shrug It Off, Battle Trance, Bloodletting, Rupture
HIGH TIER: Headbutt, Twin Strike, Molten Fist (self-exhausts = deck thin)
SOLID: Bash (only 1 needed), Juggling (needs attack density)
AVOID: Perfected Strike (anti-synergy with strike removal), True Grit (random exhaust), Anger (deck bloat)

== STRATEGIC LESSONS ==
1. REST vs UPGRADE: I rested twice but never upgraded. Should upgrade Bash (longer vuln) or Whirlwind when HP > 60%
2. CARD REMOVAL: Removing strikes is always correct early. Aim for 12-14 card deck.
3. BOSS PREP: Need 40+ HP entering boss. SteamEruption is unavoidable damage.
4. POTION USAGE: Save combat potions (energy, block) for boss fight, not regular encounters
5. ENERGY MANAGEMENT: Bloodletting is risky at low HP. Don't use it below 15 HP.
6. BLOCK PRIORITY: Against high-strength enemies, blocking is more important than damage
7. ELITE FIGHTS: Worth taking with 60%+ HP for relic rewards

== ENEMY PATTERNS ==
- Corpse Slug (Ravenous): Kill one to stun others. Worth focusing one down.
- Living Fog (Smoggy): Limits to 1 skill/turn. Prioritize attacks. Summons Gas Bombs.
- Sewer Clam (Plating): Stacking block each turn, decreases by 1. Need burst to overcome.
- Fossil Stalker (Suck): Gets strength from unblocked damage. Must block OR kill fast.
- Toadpole: Gets thorns from buff turns. Minimize multi-hit attacks against thorns.

== DECISION PRIORITIES ==
1. Always take card removal events (Precise Scissors, etc.)
2. Shop priority: Remove strike > Strong card > Relic > Potion
3. Pathing: Route through elite if HP > 60%, always hit rest before boss
4. Boss fight: Ensure survival first, damage second. Build block for final phase.
5. Don't kill boss without sufficient block for aftermath effects.
